 The Parliamentary Joint Committee is scheduled to meet today to discuss the debate that started due to the Financial Resolution and Deposit Insurance (FRDI) Bill, 2017
 is baithak main is bill ke vivaadit prastaav 'bel in' kii jaanch hogi
 On Monday, the committee is set to hold its tenth meeting
 echardiai bilke 'bel in' prastaav par is baithak main vistaar se charchaa ho sakati he
 ET quoted sources as saying that even after the government issued a clarification regarding Bell Inn, it is considered to be discussed in detail
 bataa den ki is bill ko sansadeeysanyukt samitike paas bheja gaya he
 The committee is deliberating with all stakeholders on the provisions of the FRDI bill
 samiti ko monsoon satr, 2018 ke antim din tak sansad ko apni report jamaa karne ke liye kaha gaya he
 The committee has already heard all stakeholders such as ministries, RBI, Competition Commission of India, Central Bureau of Investigation, Enforcement Directorate, industry and commerce chambers and banking representatives before its ninth meeting
 laghu udyog vikaas bank- sidbi or anya hitdharak 14 may ko samiti ke saamne apana pratinidhitiv prastut kar sakate hai
 WHAT IS FRDI BILL: Through the proposed FRDI bill, the Central Government is seeking appropriate redressal of all financial institutions such as banks, insurance companies and other financial organizations under the Code of Insolvency and Bankruptcy
 is bill ko kanoon banaakar centre sarkaar biimaar padi vittiya companiyon ko sankat se ubaarane kii koshish karegi
 The need for this bill was felt after the financial crisis of 2008 when several high-profile bankruptcy cases were reported
 centre sarkaar ne jandhan yojana or notebandi jaise faislon se lagaataar koshish kii he ki zyada se zyada log banking vyavastha ke daayre main rahen
 Due to this, it becomes very important that those who are involved in banking arrangements are guaranteed the security of their money in the event of the bank or financial institution sinking
 echardiai bill kaa pramukh praavdhanis bill main ek rejolution corporation kaa praavdhaan he jicediposit insurance or credit guarantee corporeshnaki jagah khadaa kiya jayega
 This resolution corporation will monitor the health of financial institutions and try to save them in the event of their drowning
 vahiin, jab vittiya sanstha kaa doobana tay rahegaa, to aisi sthiti main unki vittiya dendaree kaa samaadhaan karegaa
 An important function of the resolution corporation is also to provide customer codiposit insurance, although the limit of this insurance has not been fixed yet
 kyon he echardiai bill se darefardiai bill ke jarierejolution corporationako fail hone vaali sanstha ko ubaarane ke liye (bel in) kadam uthaane kaa bhi adhikaar he
 While the government invests the money of the public in a sluggish economy through bailout, it can be used to bail it out, while the bail-in is used to salvage the bank in crisis with the money of bank customers
 echardiai bill ke isi praavdhaan ke chalate aam logon main dar he ki yadi unka bank vifal hota he to unhen apni gadhi kamai se haath dhonaa pad saktaa he
 It is to be noted that according to the current provision, in the event of a bank sinking, the customer is guaranteed a mere Rs 1 lakh in the total amount deposited in his account and banks are not obliged to return the remaining money
 prastaavit echardiai bill main philhal sarkaar ne ganrti kii is rakam par abhi koi faisla nahin liya he
